runs a periodic loop to reconcile the desired state of the world with\n    46→// the actual state of the world by triggering attach detach operations.\n    47→// Note: This is distinct from the Reconciler implemented by the kubelet volume\n    48→// manager. This reconciles state for the attach/detach controller. That\n    49→// reconciles state for the kubelet volume manager.\n    50→type Reconciler interface {\n    51→\t// Starts running the reconciliation loop which executes periodically, checks\n    52→\t// if volumes that should be attached are attached and volumes that should\n    53→\t// be detached are detached. If not, it will trigger attach/detach\n    54→\t// operations to rectify.\n    55→\tRun(ctx context.Context)\n    56→}\n    57→\n    58→// NewReconciler returns a new instance of Reconciler that waits loopPeriod\n    59→// between successive executions.\n    60→// loopPeriod is the amount of time the reconciler loop waits between\n    61→// successive executions.\n    62→// maxWaitForUnmountDuration is the max amount of time the reconciler will wait\n    63→// for the volume to be safely unmounted, after this it will detach the volume\n    64→// anyway (to handle crashed/unavailable nodes). If during this time the volume\n    65→// becomes used by a new pod, the detach request will be aborted and the timer\n    66→// cleared.\n    67→func NewReconciler(\n    68→\tloopPeriod time.Duration,\n    69→\tmaxWaitForUnmountDuration time.Duration,\n    70→\tsyncDuration time.Duration,\n    71→\tdisableReconciliationSync bool,\n    72→\tdisableForceDetachOnTimeout bool,\n    73→\tdesiredStateOfWorld cache.DesiredStateOfWorld,\n    74→\tactualStateOfWorld cache.ActualStateOfWorld,\n    75→\tattacherDetacher operationexecutor.OperationExecutor,\n    76→\tnodeStatusUpdater statusupdater.NodeStatusUpdater,\n    77→\tnodeLister corelisters.NodeLister,\n    78→\trecorder record.EventRecorder) Reconciler {\n    79→\treturn &reconciler{\n    80→\t\tloopPeriod:                  loopPeriod,\n    81→\t\tmaxWaitForUnmountDuration:   maxWaitForUnmountDuration,\n    82→\t\tsyncDuration:                syncDuration,\n    83→\t\tdisableReconciliationSync:   disableReconciliationSync,\n    84→\t\tdisableForceDetachOnTimeout: disableForceDetachOnTimeout,\n    85→\t\tdesiredStateOfWorld:         desiredStateOfWorld,\n    86→\t\tactualStateOfWorld:          actualStateOfWorld,\n    87→\t\tattacherDetacher:            attacherDetacher,\n    88→\t\tnodeStatusUpdater:           nodeStatusUpdater,\n    89→\t\tnodeLister:                  nodeLister,\n    90→\t\ttimeOfLastSync:              time.Now(),\n    91→\t\trecorder:                    recorder,\n    92→\t}\n    93→}\n    94→\n    95→type reconciler struct {\n    96→\tloopPeriod                  time.Duration\n    97→\tmaxWaitForUnmountDuration   time.Duration\n    98→\tsyncDuration                time.Duration\n    99→\tdesiredStateOfWorld         cache.DesiredStateOfWorld\n   100→\tactualStateOfWorld          cache.ActualStateOfWorld\n   101→\tattacherDetacher            operationexecutor.OperationExecutor\n   102→\tnodeStatusUpdater           statusupdater.NodeStatusUpdater\n   103→\tnodeLister                  corelisters.NodeLister\n   104→\ttimeOfLastSync              time.Time\n   105→\tdisableReconciliationSync   bool\n   106→\tdisableForceDetachOnTimeout bool\n   107→\trecorder                    record.EventRecorder\n   108→}\n   109→\n   110→func (rc *reconciler) Run(ctx context.Context) {\n   111→\twait.UntilWithContext(ctx, rc.reconciliationLoopFunc(ctx), rc.loopPeriod)\n   112→}\n   113→\n   114→// reconciliationLoopFunc this can be disabled via cli option disableReconciliation.\n   115→// It periodically checks whether the attached volumes from actual state\n   116→// are still attached to the node and update the status if they are not.\n   117→func (rc *reconciler) reconciliationLoopFunc(ctx context.Context) func(context.Context) {\n   118→\treturn func(ctx context.Context) {\n   119→\n   120→\t\trc.reconcile(ctx)\n   121→\t\tlogger := klog.FromContext(ctx)\n   122→\t\tif rc.disableReconciliationSync {\n   123→\t\t\tlogger.V(5).Info(\"Skipping reconciling attached volumes still attached since it is disabled via the command line\")\n   124→\t\t} else if rc.syncDuration < time.Second {\n   125→\t\t\tlogger.V(5).Info(\"Skipping reconciling attached volumes still attached since it is set to less than one second via the command line\")\n   126→\t\t} else if time.Since(rc.timeOfLastSync) > rc.syncDuration {\n   127→\t\t\tlogger.V(5).Info(\"Starting reconciling attached volumes still attached\")\n   128→\t\t\trc.sync()\n   129→\t\t}\n   130→\t}\n   131→}\n   132→\n   133→func (rc *reconciler) sync() {\n   134→\tdefer rc.updateSyncTime()\n   135→\trc.syncStates()\n   136→}\n   137→\n   138→func (rc *reconciler) updateSyncTime() {\n   139→\trc.timeOfLastSync = time.Now()\n   140→}\n   141→\n   142→func (rc *reconciler) syncStates() {\n   143→\tvolumesPerNode := rc.actualStateOfWorld.GetAttachedVolumesPerNode()\n   144→\trc.attacherDetacher.VerifyVolumesAreAttached(volumesPerNode, rc.actualStateOfWorld)\n   145→}\n   146→\n   147→// hasOutOfServiceTaint returns true if the node has out-of-service taint present.\n   148→func (rc *reconciler) hasOutOfServiceTaint(nodeName types.NodeName) (bool, error) {\n   149→\tnode, err := rc.nodeLister.Get(string(nodeName))\n   150→\tif err != nil {\n   151→\t\treturn false, err\n   152→\t}\n   153→\treturn taints.TaintKeyExists(node.Spec.Taints, v1.TaintNodeOutOfService), nil\n   154→}\n   155→\n   156→// nodeIsHealthy returns true if the node looks healthy.\n   157→func (rc *reconciler) nodeIsHealthy(nodeName types.NodeName) (bool, error) {\n   158→\tnode, err := rc.nodeLister.Get(string(nodeName))\n   159→\tif err != nil {\n   160→\t\treturn false, err\n   161→\t}\n   162→\treturn nodeutil.IsNodeReady(node), nil\n   163→}\n   164→\n   165→func (rc *reconciler) reconcile(ctx context.Context) {\n   166→\t// Detaches are triggered before attaches so that volumes referenced by\n   167→\t// pods that are rescheduled to a different node are detached first.\n   168→\n   169→\t// Ensure volumes that should be detached are detached.\n   170→\tlogger := klog.FromContext(ctx)\n   171→\tfor _, attachedVolume := range rc.actualStateOfWorld.GetAttachedVolumes() {\n   172→\t\tif !rc.desiredStateOfWorld.VolumeExists(\n   173→\t\t\tattachedVolume.VolumeName, attachedVolume.NodeName) {\n   174→\n   175→\t\t\t// Check whether there already exist an operation pending, and don't even\n   176→\t\t\t// try to start an operation if there is already one running.\n   177→\t\t\t// This check must be done before we do any other checks, as otherwise the other checks\n   178→\t\t\t// may pass while at the same time the volume leaves the pending state, resulting in\n   179→\t\t\t// double detach attempts\n   180→\t\t\t// The operation key format is different depending on whether the volume\n   181→\t\t\t// allows multi attach across different nodes.\n   182→\t\t\tif util.IsMultiAttachAllowed(attachedVolume.VolumeSpec) {\n   183→\t\t\t\tif !rc.attacherDetacher.IsOperationSafeToRetry(attachedVolume.VolumeName, \"\" /* podName */, attachedVolume.NodeName, operationexecutor.DetachOperationName) {\n   184→\t\t\t\t\tlogger.V(10).Info(\"Operation for volume is already running or still in exponential backoff for node. Can't start detach\", \"node\", klog.KRef(\"\", string(attachedVolume.NodeName)), \"volumeName\", attachedVolume.VolumeName)\n   185→\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   186→\t\t\t\t}\n   187→\t\t\t} else {\n   188→\t\t\t\tif !rc.attacherDetacher.IsOperationSafeToRetry(attachedVolume.VolumeName, \"\" /* podName */, \"\" /* nodeName */, operationexecutor.DetachOperationName) {\n   189→\t\t\t\t\tlogger.V(10).Info(\"Operation for volume is already running or still in exponential backoff in the cluster. Can't start detach for node\", \"node\", klog.KRef(\"\", string(attachedVolume.NodeName)), \"volumeName\", attachedVolume.VolumeName)\n   190→\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   191→\t\t\t\t}\n   192→\t\t\t}\n   193→\n   194→\t\t\t// Because the detach operation updates the ActualStateOfWorld before\n   195→\t\t\t// marking itself complete, it's possible for the volume to be removed\n   196→\t\t\t// from the ActualStateOfWorld between the GetAttachedVolumes() check\n   197→\t\t\t// and the IsOperationSafeToRetry() check above.\n   198→\t\t\t// Check the ActualStateOfWorld again to avoid issuing an unnecessary\n   199→\t\t\t// detach.\n   200→\t\t\t// See https://github.com/kubernetes/kubernetes/issues/93902\n   201→\t\t\tattachState := rc.actualStateOfWorld.GetAttachState(attachedVolume.VolumeName, attachedVolume.NodeName)\n   202→\t\t\tif attachState == cache.AttachStateDetached {\n   203→\t\t\t\tlogger.V(5).Info(\"Volume detached--skipping\", \"node\", klog.KRef(\"\", string(attachedVolume.NodeName)), \"volumeName\", attachedVolume.VolumeName)\n   204→\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   205→\t\t\t}\n   206→\n   207→\t\t\t// Set the detach request time\n   208→\t\t\telapsedTime, err := rc.actualStateOfWorld.SetDetachRequestTime(logger, attachedVolume.VolumeName, attachedVolume.NodeName)\n   209→\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   210→\t\t\t\tlogger.Error(err, \"Cannot trigger detach because it fails to set detach request time with error\")\n   211→\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   212→\t\t\t}\n   213→\t\t\t// Check whether the umount drain timer expired\n   214→\t\t\tmaxWaitForUnmountDurationExpired := elapsedTime > rc.maxWaitForUnmountDuration\n   215→\n   216→\t\t\tisHealthy, err := rc.nodeIsHealthy(attachedVolume.NodeName)\n   217→\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   218→\t\t\t\tlogger.Error(err, \"Failed to get health of node\", \"node\", klog.KRef(\"\", string(attachedVolume.NodeName)))\n   219→\t\t\t}\n   220→\n   221→\t\t\t// Force detach volumes from unhealthy nodes after maxWaitForUnmountDuration if force detach is enabled\n   222→\t\t\t// Ensure that the timeout condition checks this correctly so that the correct metric is updated below\n   223→\t\t\tforceDetatchTimeoutExpired := maxWaitForUnmountDurationExpired && !rc.disableForceDetachOnTimeout\n   224→\t\t\tif maxWaitForUnmountDurationExpired && rc.disableForceDetachOnTimeout {\n   225→\t\t\t\tlogger.V(5).Info(\"Drain timeout expired for volume but disableForceDetachOnTimeout was set\", \"node\", klog.KRef(\"\", string(attachedVolume.NodeName)), \"volumeName\", attachedVolume.VolumeName)\n   226→\t\t\t}\n   227→\t\t\tforceDetach := !isHealthy && forceDetatchTimeoutExpired\n   228→\n   229→\t\t\thasOutOfServiceTaint, err := rc.hasOutOfServiceTaint(attachedVolume.NodeName)\n   230→\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   231→\t\t\t\tlogger.Error(err, \"Failed to get taint specs for node\", \"node\", klog.KRef(\"\", string(attachedVolume.NodeName)))\n   232→\t\t\t}\n   233→\n   234→\t\t\t// Check whether volume is still mounted. Skip detach if it is still mounted unless we have\n   235→\t\t\t// decided to force detach or the node has `node.kubernetes.io/out-of-service` taint.\n   236→\t\t\tif attachedVolume.MountedByNode && !forceDetach && !hasOutOfServiceTaint {\n   237→\t\t\t\tlogger.V(5).Info(\"Cannot detach volume because it is still mounted\", \"node\", klog.KRef(\"\", string(attachedVolume.NodeName)), \"volumeName\", attachedVolume.VolumeName)\n   238→\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   239→\t\t\t}\n   240→\n   241→\t\t\t// Before triggering volume detach, mark volume as detached and update the node status\n   242→\t\t\t// If it fails to update node status, skip detach volume\n   243→\t\t\t// If volume detach operation fails, the volume needs to be added back to report as attached so that node status\n   244→\t\t\t// has the correct volume attachment information.\n   245→\t\t\terr = rc.actualStateOfWorld.RemoveVolumeFromReportAsAttached(attachedVolume.VolumeName, attachedVolume.NodeName)\n   246→\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   247→\t\t\t\tlogger.V(5).Info(\"RemoveVolumeFromReportAsAttached failed while removing volume from node\",\n   248→\t\t\t\t\t\"node\", klog.KRef(\"\", string(attachedVolume.NodeName)),\n   249→\t\t\t\t\t\"volumeName\", attachedVolume.VolumeName,\n   250→\t\t\t\t\t\"err\", err)\n   251→\t\t\t}\n   252→\n   253→\t\t\t// Update Node Status to indicate volume is no longer safe to mount.\n   254→\t\t\terr = rc.nodeStatusUpdater.UpdateNodeStatusForNode(logger, attachedVolume.NodeName)\n   255→\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   256→\t\t\t\t// Skip detaching this volume if unable to update node status\n   257→\t\t\t\tlogger.Error(err, \"UpdateNodeStatusForNode failed while attempting to report volume as attached\", \"node\", klog.KRef(\"\", string(attachedVolume.NodeName)), \"volumeName\", attachedVolume.VolumeName)\n   258→\t\t\t\t// Add volume back to ReportAsAttached if UpdateNodeStatusForNode call failed so that node status updater will add it back to VolumeAttached list.\n   259→\t\t\t\t// It is needed here too because DetachVolume is not call actually and we keep the data consistency for every reconcile.\n   260→\t\t\t\trc.actualStateOfWorld.AddVolumeToReportAsAttached(logger, attachedVolume.VolumeName, attachedVolume.NodeName)\n   261→\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   262→\t\t\t}\n   263→\n   264→\t\t\t// Trigger rc.attacherDetacher.DetachVolume(logger, attachedVolume.AttachedVolume, verifySafeToDetach, rc.actualStateOfWorld)\n   273→\t\t\tif err == nil {\n   274→\t\t\t\tif verifySafeToDetach { // normal 279→\t\t\t\t\t\tlogger.Info(\"attacherDetacher.DetachVolume started: this volume is not safe to detach, but maxWaitForUnmountDuration expired, force detaching\",\n   280→\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\"duration\", rc.maxWaitForUnmountDuration,\n   281→\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\"node\", klog.KRef(\"\", string(attachedVolume.NodeName)),\n   282→\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\"volumeName\", attachedVolume.VolumeName)\n   283→\t\t\t\t\t} else {\n   284→\t\t\t\t\t\tmetrics.RecordForcedDetachMetric(metrics.ForceDetachReasonOutOfService)\n   285→\t\t\t\t\t\tlogger.Info(\"attacherDetacher.DetachVolume started: node has out-of-service taint, force detaching\",\n   286→\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\"node\", klog.KRef(\"\", string(attachedVolume.NodeName)),\n   287→\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\"volumeName\", attachedVolume.VolumeName)\n   288→\t\t\t\t\t}\n   289→\t\t\t\t}\n   290→\t\t\t}\n   291→\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   292→\t\t\t\t// Add volume back to ReportAsAttached if DetachVolume call failed so that node status updater will add it back to VolumeAttached list.\n   293→\t\t\t\t// This function is also called during executing the volume detach operation in operation_generoator.\n   294→\t\t\t\t// It is needed here too because DetachVolume call might fail before executing the actual operation in operation_executor (e.g., cannot find volume plugin etc.)\n   295→\t\t\t\trc.actualStateOfWorld.AddVolumeToReportAsAttached(logger, attachedVolume.VolumeName, attachedVolume.NodeName)\n   296→\n   297→\t\t\t\tif !exponentialbackoff.IsExponentialBackoff(err) {\n   298→\t\t\t\t\t// Ignore exponentialbackoff.IsExponentialBackoff errors, they are expected.\n   299→\t\t\t\t\t// Log all other errors.\n   300→\t\t\t\t\tlogger.Error(err, \"attacherDetacher.DetachVolume failed to start\", \"node\", klog.KRef(\"\", string(attachedVolume.NodeName)), \"volumeName\", attachedVolume.VolumeName)\n   301→\t\t\t\t}\n   302→\t\t\t}\n   303→\t\t}\n   304→\t}\n   305→\n   306→\trc.attachDesiredVolumes(logger)\n   307→\n   308→\t// Update Node Status\n   309→\terr := rc.nodeStatusUpdater.UpdateNodeStatuses(logger)\n   310→\tif err != nil {\n   311→\t\tlogger.Info(\"UpdateNodeStatuses failed\", \"err\", err)\n   312→\t}\n   313→}\n   314→\n   315→func (rc *reconciler) attachDesiredVolumes(logger klog.Logger) {\n   316→\t// Ensure volumes that should be attached are attached.\n   317→\tfor _, volumeToAttach := range rc.desiredStateOfWorld.GetVolumesToAttach() {\n   318→\t\tif util.IsMultiAttachAllowed(volumeToAttach.VolumeSpec) {\n   319→\t\t\t// Don't even try to start an operation if there is already one running for the given volume and node.\n   320→\t\t\tif rc.attacherDetacher.IsOperationPending(volumeToAttach.VolumeName, \"\" /* podName */, volumeToAttach.NodeName) {\n   321→\t\t\t\tlogger.V(10).Info(\"Operation for volume is already running for node. Can't start attach\", \"node\", klog.KRef(\"\", string(volumeToAttach.NodeName)), \"volumeName\", volumeToAttach.VolumeName)\n   322→\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   323→\t\t\t}\n   324→\t\t} else {\n   325→\t\t\t// Don't even try to start an operation if there is already one running for the given volume\n   326→\t\t\tif rc.attacherDetacher.IsOperationPending(volumeToAttach.VolumeName, \"\" /* podName */, \"\" /* nodeName */) {\n   327→\t\t\t\tlogger.V(10).Info(\"Operation for volume is already running. Can't start attach for node\", \"node\", klog.KRef(\"\", string(volumeToAttach.NodeName)), \"volumeNames\", volumeToAttach.VolumeName)\n   328→\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   329→\t\t\t}\n   330→\t\t}\n   331→\n   332→\t\t// Because the attach operation updates the ActualStateOfWorld before\n   333→\t\t// marking itself complete, IsOperationPending() must be checked before\n   334→\t\t// GetAttachState() to guarantee the ActualStateOfWorld is\n   335→\t\t// up-to-date when it's read.\n   336→\t\t// See https://github.com/kubernetes/kubernetes/issues/93902\n   337→\t\tattachState := 351→\t\t\t\t}\n   352→\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   353→\t\t\t}\n   354→\t\t}\n   355→\n   356→\t\t// Volume/Node doesn't exist, spawn a goroutine to attach it\n   357→\t\tlogger.V(5).Info(\"Starting {\n   360→\t\t\tlogger.Info(\"attacherDetacher.AttachVolume started\", \"volumeName\", volumeToAttach.VolumeName, \"nodeName\", volumeToAttach.NodeName, \"scheduledPods\", errors, they are expected.\n   364→\t\t\t// Log all other errors.\n   365→\t\t\tlogger.Error(err, \"attacherDetacher.AttachVolume failed to start\", \"volumeName\", volumeToAttach.VolumeName, logs situation that a volume that\n   371→// should be attached to a node is already attached to different node(s).\n   372→func (rc *reconciler) reportMultiAttachError(logger klog.Logger, volumeToAttach cache.VolumeToAttach, nodes []types.NodeName) {\n   373→\t// Filter out the current node from list of nodes where the volume is\n   374→\t// attached.\n   375→\t// Some methods need []string, some other needs []NodeName, collect both.\n   376→\t// In theory, these arrays should have always only one element - the\n   377→\t// controller does not allow more than one attachment. But use array just\n   378→\t// in case...\n   379→\totherNodes := []types.NodeName{}\n   380→\totherNodesStr := []string{}\n   381→\tfor _, node := range nodes {\n   382→\t\tif node != volumeToAttach.NodeName {\n   383→\t\t\totherNodes = append(otherNodes, node)\n   384→\t\t\totherNodesStr = append(otherNodesStr, string(node))\n   385→\t\t}\n   386→\t}\n   387→\n   388→\t// Get list of pods that use the volume on the other nodes.\n   389→\tpods := rc.desiredStateOfWorld.GetVolumePodsOnNodes(otherNodes, volumeToAttach.VolumeName)\n   390→\tif len(pods) == 0 {\n   391→\t\t// We did not find any pods that requests the volume. The pod must have been deleted already.\n   392→\t\tsimpleMsg, _ := volumeToAttach.GenerateMsg(\"Multi-Attach error\", \"Volume is already exclusively attached to one node and can't be attached to another\")\n   393→\t\tfor _, pod := range volumeToAttach.ScheduledPods {\n   394→\t\t\trc.recorder.Eventf(pod, v1.EventTypeWarning, kevents.FailedAttachVolume, simpleMsg)\n   395→\t\t}\n   396→\t\t// Log detailed message to system admin\n   397→\t\tlogger.Info(\"Multi-Attach error: volume is already exclusively attached and can't be attached to another node\", \"attachedTo\", otherNodesStr, \"volume\", volumeToAttach)\n   398→\t\treturn\n   399→\t}\n   400→\n   401→\t// There are pods that require the volume and run on another node. Typically\n   402→\t// it's user error, e.g. a ReplicaSet uses a PVC and has >1 replicas. Let\n   403→\t// the user know what pods are blocking the volume.\n   404→\tfor _, scheduledPod := range volumeToAttach.ScheduledPods {\n   405→\t\t// Each scheduledPod must get a custom message. They can run in\n   406→\t\t// different namespaces and user of a namespace should not see names of\n   407→\t\t// pods in other namespaces.\n   408→\t\tlocalPodNames := []string{} // Names of pods in scheduledPods's namespace\n   409→\t\totherPods := 0              // Count of pods in other namespaces\n   410→\t\tfor _, pod := range pods {\n   411→\t\t\tif pod.Namespace == scheduledPod.Namespace {\n   412→\t\t\t\tlocalPodNames = append(localPodNames, pod.Name)\n   413→\t\t\t} else {\n   414→\t\t\t\totherPods++\n   415→\t\t\t}\n   416→\t\t}\n   417→\n   418→\t\tvar msg string\n   419→\t\tif len(localPodNames) > 0 {\n   420→\t\t\tmsg = fmt.Sprintf(\"Volume is already used by pod(s) %s\", strings.Join(localPodNames, \", \"))\n   421→\t\t\tif otherPods > 0 {\n   422→\t\t\t\tmsg = fmt.Sprintf(\"%s and %d pod(s) in different namespaces\", msg, otherPods)\n   423→\t\t\t}\n   424→\t\t} else {\n   425→\t\t\t// No local pods, there are pods only in different namespaces.\n   426→\t\t\tmsg = fmt.Sprintf(\"Volume is already used by %d pod(s) in different namespaces\", otherPods)\n   427→\t\t}\n   428→\t\tsimpleMsg, _ := volumeToAttach.GenerateMsg(\"Multi-Attach error\", msg)\n   429→\t\trc.recorder.Eventf(scheduledPod, v1.EventTypeWarning, kevents.FailedAttachVolume, simpleMsg)\n   430→\t}\n   431→\n   432→\t// Log all pods for system admin\n   433→\tlogger.Info(\"Multi-Attach error: volume is already used by pods\", \"pods\", klog.KObjSlice(pods), \"attachedTo\", otherNodesStr, \"volume\", volumeToAttach)\n   434→}\n   435→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware. (\n\t\"context\"\n\t\"fmt\"\n\t\"strings\"\n\t\"time\"\n\n\tv1 \"k8s.io/api/core/v1\"\n\t\"k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/types\"\n\t\"k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/util/wait\"\n\tcorelisters \"k8s.io/kubernetes/pkg/kubelet/events\"\n\t\"k8s.io/kubernetes/pkg/util/goroutinemap/exponentialbackoff\"\n\tnodeutil \"k8s.io/kubernetes/pkg/util/node\"\n\t\"k8s.io/kubernetes/pkg/util/taints\"\n\t\"k8s.io/kubernetes/pkg/volume/util\"\n\t\"k8s.io/kubernetes/pkg/volume/util/operationexecutor\"\n)\n\n// Reconciler runs a periodic loop to reconcile the desired state of the world with\n// the actual state of the world by triggering attach detach operations.\n// Note: This is distinct from the Reconciler implemented by the kubelet volume\n// manager. This reconciles state for the attach/detach controller. That\n// reconciles state for the kubelet volume manager.\ntype Reconciler interface {\n\t// Starts running the reconciliation loop which executes periodically, checks\n\t// if volumes that should be attached are attached and volumes that should\n\t// be detached are detached. If not, it will trigger attach/detach\n\t// operations to rectify.\n\tRun(ctx context.Context)\n}\n\n// NewReconciler returns a new instance of Reconciler that waits loopPeriod\n// between successive executions.\n// loopPeriod is the amount of time the reconciler loop waits between\n// successive executions.\n// maxWaitForUnmountDuration is the max amount of time the reconciler will wait\n// for the volume to be safely unmounted, after this it will detach the volume\n// anyway (to handle crashed/unavailable nodes). If during this time the volume\n// becomes used by a new pod, the detach request will be aborted and the timer\n// cleared.\nfunc NewReconciler(\n\tloopPeriod time.Duration,\n\tmaxWaitForUnmountDuration time.Duration,\n\tsyncDuration time.Duration,\n\tdisableReconciliationSync bool,\n\tdisableForceDetachOnTimeout bool,\n\tdesiredStateOfWorld cache.DesiredStateOfWorld,\n\tactualStateOfWorld cache.ActualStateOfWorld,\n\tattacherDetacher operationexecutor.OperationExecutor,\n\tnodeStatusUpdater statusupdater.NodeStatusUpdater,\n\tnodeLister corelisters.NodeLister,\n\trecorder record.EventRecorder) Reconciler {\n\treturn &reconciler{\n\t\tloopPeriod:                  loopPeriod,\n\t\tmaxWaitForUnmountDuration:   maxWaitForUnmountDuration,\n\t\tsyncDuration:                syncDuration,\n\t\tdisableReconciliationSync:   disableReconciliationSync,\n\t\tdisableForceDetachOnTimeout: disableForceDetachOnTimeout,\n\t\tdesiredStateOfWorld:         desiredStateOfWorld,\n\t\tactualStateOfWorld:          actualStateOfWorld,\n\t\tattacherDetacher:            attacherDetacher,\n\t\tnodeStatusUpdater:           nodeStatusUpdater,\n\t\tnodeLister:                  nodeLister,\n\t\ttimeOfLastSync:              time.Now(),\n\t\trecorder:                    recorder,\n\t}\n}\n\ntype reconciler struct {\n\tloopPeriod                  time.Duration\n\tmaxWaitForUnmountDuration   time.Duration\n\tsyncDuration                time.Duration\n\tdesiredStateOfWorld         cache.DesiredStateOfWorld\n\tactualStateOfWorld          cache.ActualStateOfWorld\n\tattacherDetacher            operationexecutor.OperationExecutor\n\tnodeStatusUpdater           statusupdater.NodeStatusUpdater\n\tnodeLister                  corelisters.NodeLister\n\ttimeOfLastSync              time.Time\n\tdisableReconciliationSync   bool\n\tdisableForceDetachOnTimeout bool\n\trecorder                    record.EventRecorder\n}\n\nfunc (rc *reconciler) Run(ctx context.Context) {\n\twait.UntilWithContext(ctx, rc.reconciliationLoopFunc(ctx), rc.loopPeriod)\n}\n\n// reconciliationLoopFunc this can be disabled via cli option disableReconciliation.\n// It periodically checks whether the attached volumes from actual state\n// are still attached to the node and update the status if they are not.\nfunc (rc *reconciler) reconciliationLoopFunc(ctx context.Context) func(context.Context) {\n\treturn func(ctx context.Context) {\n\n\t\trc.reconcile(ctx)\n\t\tlogger := klog.FromContext(ctx)\n\t\tif rc.disableReconciliationSync {\n\t\t\tlogger.V(5).Info(\"Skipping reconciling attached volumes still attached since it is disabled via the command line\")\n\t\t} else if rc.syncDuration < time.Second {\n\t\t\tlogger.V(5).Info(\"Skipping reconciling attached volumes still attached since it is set to less than one second via the command line\")\n\t\t} else if time.Since(rc.timeOfLastSync) > rc.syncDuration {\n\t\t\tlogger.V(5).Info(\"Starting reconciling attached volumes still attached\")\n\t\t\trc.sync()\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc (rc *reconciler) sync() {\n\tdefer rc.updateSyncTime()\n\trc.syncStates()\n}\n\nfunc (rc *reconciler) updateSyncTime() {\n\trc.timeOfLastSync = time.Now()\n}\n\nfunc (rc *reconciler) syncStates() {\n\tvolumesPerNode := rc.actualStateOfWorld.GetAttachedVolumesPerNode()\n\trc.attacherDetacher.VerifyVolumesAreAttached(volumesPerNode, rc.actualStateOfWorld)\n}\n\n// hasOutOfServiceTaint returns true if the node has out-of-service taint present.\nfunc (rc *reconciler) hasOutOfServiceTaint(nodeName types.NodeName) (bool, error) {\n\tnode, err := rc.nodeLister.Get(string(nodeName))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn false, err\n\t}\n\treturn taints.TaintKeyExists(node.Spec.Taints, v1.TaintNodeOutOfService), nil\n}\n\n// nodeIsHealthy returns true if the node looks healthy.\nfunc (rc *reconciler) nodeIsHealthy(nodeName types.NodeName) (bool, error) {\n\tnode, err := rc.nodeLister.Get(string(nodeName))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn false, err\n\t}\n\treturn nodeutil.IsNodeReady(node), nil\n}\n\nfunc (rc *reconciler) reconcile(ctx context.Context) {\n\t// Detaches are triggered before attaches so that volumes referenced by\n\t// pods that are rescheduled to a different node are detached first.\n\n\t// Ensure volumes that should be detached are detached.\n\tlogger := klog.FromContext(ctx)\n\tfor _, attachedVolume := range rc.actualStateOfWorld.GetAttachedVolumes() {\n\t\tif !rc.desiredStateOfWorld.VolumeExists(\n\t\t\tattachedVolume.VolumeName, attachedVolume.NodeName) {\n\n\t\t\t// Check whether there already exist an operation pending, and don't even\n\t\t\t// try to start an operation if there is already one running.\n\t\t\t// This check must be done before we do any other checks, as otherwise the other checks\n\t\t\t// may pass while at the same time the volume leaves the pending state, resulting in\n\t\t\t// double detach attempts\n\t\t\t// The operation key format is different depending on whether the volume\n\t\t\t// allows multi attach across different nodes.\n\t\t\tif util.IsMultiAttachAllowed(attachedVolume.VolumeSpec) {\n\t\t\t\tif !rc.attacherDetacher.IsOperationSafeToRetry(attachedVolume.VolumeName, \"\" /* podName */, attachedVolume.NodeName, operationexecutor.DetachOperationName) {\n\t\t\t\t\tlogger.V(10).Info(\"Operation for volume is already running or still in exponential backoff for node. Can't start detach\", \"node\", klog.KRef(\"\", string(attachedVolume.NodeName)), \"volumeName\", attachedVolume.VolumeName)\n\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\tif !rc.attacherDetacher.IsOperationSafeToRetry(attachedVolume.VolumeName, \"\" /* podName */, \"\" /* nodeName */, operationexecutor.DetachOperationName) {\n\t\t\t\t\tlogger.V(10).Info(\"Operation for volume is already running or still in exponential backoff in the cluster. Can't start detach for node\", \"node\", klog.KRef(\"\", string(attachedVolume.NodeName)), \"volumeName\", attachedVolume.VolumeName)\n\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t// Because the detach operation updates the ActualStateOfWorld before\n\t\t\t// marking itself complete, it's possible for the volume to be removed\n\t\t\t// from the ActualStateOfWorld between the GetAttachedVolumes() check\n\t\t\t// and the IsOperationSafeToRetry() check above.\n\t\t\t// Check the ActualStateOfWorld again to avoid issuing an unnecessary\n\t\t\t// detach.\n\t\t\t// See https://github.com/kubernetes/kubernetes/issues/93902\n\t\t\tattachState := rc.actualStateOfWorld.GetAttachState(attachedVolume.VolumeName, attachedVolume.NodeName)\n\t\t\tif attachState == cache.AttachStateDetached {\n\t\t\t\tlogger.V(5).Info(\"Volume detached--skipping\", \"node\", klog.KRef(\"\", string(attachedVolume.NodeName)), \"volumeName\", attachedVolume.VolumeName)\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t// Set the detach request time\n\t\t\telapsedTime, err := rc.actualStateOfWorld.SetDetachRequestTime(logger, attachedVolume.VolumeName, attachedVolume.NodeName)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\tlogger.Error(err, \"Cannot trigger detach because it fails to set detach request time with error\")\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t// Check whether the umount drain timer expired\n\t\t\tmaxWaitForUnmountDurationExpired := elapsedTime > rc.maxWaitForUnmountDuration\n\n\t\t\tisHealthy, err := rc.nodeIsHealthy(attachedVolume.NodeName)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\tlogger.Error(err, \"Failed to get health of node\", \"node\", klog.KRef(\"\", string(attachedVolume.NodeName)))\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t// Force detach volumes from unhealthy nodes after maxWaitForUnmountDuration if force detach is enabled\n\t\t\t// Ensure that the timeout condition checks this correctly so that the correct metric is updated below\n\t\t\tforceDetatchTimeoutExpired := maxWaitForUnmountDurationExpired && !rc.disableForceDetachOnTimeout\n\t\t\tif maxWaitForUnmountDurationExpired && rc.disableForceDetachOnTimeout {\n\t\t\t\tlogger.V(5).Info(\"Drain timeout expired for volume but disableForceDetachOnTimeout was set\", \"node\", klog.KRef(\"\", string(attachedVolume.NodeName)), \"volumeName\", attachedVolume.VolumeName)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tforceDetach := !isHealthy && forceDetatchTimeoutExpired\n\n\t\t\thasOutOfServiceTaint, err := attachedVolume.VolumeName)\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t// Before triggering volume detach, mark volume as detached and update the node status\n\t\t\t// If it fails to update node status, skip information.\n\t\t\terr = rc.actualStateOfWorld.RemoveVolumeFromReportAsAttached(attachedVolume.VolumeName, attachedVolume.NodeName)\n\t\t\tif err != nil attachedVolume.VolumeName)\n\t\t\t\t// Add volume back to ReportAsAttached if UpdateNodeStatusForNode call failed so that node status updater will add it back to VolumeAttached list.\n\t\t\t\t// It is needed here too because DetachVolume is not call actually and we keep the data consistency for every reconcile.\n\t\t\t\trc.actualStateOfWorld.AddVolumeToReportAsAttached(logger, true, skip verifySafeToDetach check\n\t\t\t// If the node has node.kubernetes.io/out-of-service taint with NoExecute effect, skip verifySafeToDetach check\n\t\t\tlogger.V(5).Info(\"Starting {\n\t\t\t\tlogger.V(4).Info(\"node has out-of-service taint\", \"node\", klog.KRef(\"\", string(attachedVolume.NodeName)))\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tverifySafeToDetach := !(forceDetatchTimeoutExpired || hasOutOfServiceTaint)\n\t\t\terr = rc.attacherDetacher.DetachVolume(logger, attachedVolume.AttachedVolume, verifySafeToDetach, rc.actualStateOfWorld)\n\t\t\tif err == nil {\n\t\t\t\tif verifySafeToDetach { // normal detach\n\t\t\t\t\tlogger.Info(\"attacherDetacher.DetachVolume started\", \"node\", klog.KRef(\"\", string(attachedVolume.NodeName)), \"volumeName\", attachedVolume.VolumeName)\n\t\t\t\t} else { // force detach\n\t\t\t\t\tif forceDetatchTimeoutExpired if there is already one running for the given volume and node.\n\t\t\tif rc.attacherDetacher.IsOperationPending(volumeToAttach.VolumeName, \"\" /* podName */, volumeToAttach.NodeName) {\n\t\t\t\tlogger.V(10).Info(\"Operation for volume is already running for node. Can't start attach\", \"node\", klog.KRef(\"\", string(volumeToAttach.NodeName)), \"volumeName\", volumeToAttach.VolumeName)\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t// Don't even try to start an operation if there is already one running for the given volume\n\t\t\tif rc.attacherDetacher.IsOperationPending(volumeToAttach.VolumeName, \"\" /* podName */, \"\" /* nodeName */) {\n\t\t\t\tlogger.V(10).Info(\"Operation for volume is already running. up-to-date when it's read.\n\t\t// See https://github.com/kubernetes/kubernetes/issues/93902\n\t\tattachState := rc.actualStateOfWorld.GetAttachState(volumeToAttach.VolumeName, already attached to different node(s).\nfunc (rc *reconciler) reportMultiAttachError(logger klog.Logger, volumeToAttach cache.VolumeToAttach, nodes []types.NodeName) {\n\t// Filter out the current node from list of nodes where the volume is\n\t// attached.\n\t// Some methods need []string, some other needs []NodeName, collect both.\n\t// In theory, these arrays should have always only one element - the\n\t// controller does not allow more than one attachment. But use array just\n\t// in case...\n\totherNodes := []types.NodeName{}\n\totherNodesStr := []string{}\n\tfor _, node := range nodes {\n\t\tif node != volumeToAttach.NodeName {\n\t\t\totherNodes = append(otherNodes, node)\n\t\t\totherNodesStr = append(otherNodesStr, string(node))\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Get list of pods that use the volume on the other nodes.\n\tpods := rc.desiredStateOfWorld.GetVolumePodsOnNodes(otherNodes, volumeToAttach.VolumeName)\n\tif len(pods) == 0 {\n\t\t// We did not find any pods that requests the volume. The pod must have been deleted already.\n\t\tsimpleMsg, _ := volumeToAttach.GenerateMsg(\"Multi-Attach error\", \"Volume is already exclusively attached to one node and can't be attached to another\")\n\t\tfor _, pod := range volumeToAttach.ScheduledPods {\n\t\t\trc.recorder.Eventf(pod, v1.EventTypeWarning, kevents.FailedAttachVolume, simpleMsg)\n\t\t}\n\t\t// Log detailed message to system admin\n\t\tlogger.Info(\"Multi-Attach error: volume is already exclusively attached and can't be attached to another node\", \"attachedTo\", otherNodesStr, \"volume\", volumeToAttach)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// There are pods that require the volume and run on another node. Typically\n\t// it's user error, e.g. a ReplicaSet uses a PVC and has >1 replicas. Let\n\t// the user know what pods are blocking the volume.\n\tfor _, scheduledPod := range volumeToAttach.ScheduledPods {\n\t\t// Each scheduledPod must get a custom message. They can run in\n\t\t// different namespaces and user of a namespace should not see names of\n\t\t// pods in other namespaces.\n\t\tlocalPodNames := []string{} // Names of pods in scheduledPods's namespace\n\t\totherPods := 0              // Count of pods in other namespaces\n\t\tfor _, pod := range pods {\n\t\t\tif pod.Namespace == scheduledPod.Namespace {\n\t\t\t\tlocalPodNames = append(localPodNames, pod.Name)\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\totherPods++\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tvar msg string\n\t\tif len(localPodNames) > 0 {\n\t\t\tmsg = fmt.Sprintf(\"Volume is already used by pod(s) %s\", strings.Join(localPodNames, \", \"))\n\t\t\tif otherPods > 0 {\n\t\t\t\tmsg = fmt.Sprintf(\"%s and %d pod(s) in different namespaces\", msg, otherPods)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t// No local pods, there are pods only in different namespaces.\n\t\t\tmsg = fmt.Sprintf(\"Volume is already used by %d pod(s) in different namespaces\", otherPods)\n\t\t}\n\t\tsimpleMsg, _ := volumeToAttach.GenerateMsg(\"Multi-Attach error\", msg)\n\t\trc.recorder.Eventf(scheduledPod, v1.EventTypeWarning, kevents.FailedAttachVolume, simpleMsg)\n\t}\n\n\t// Log all pods for system admin\n\tlogger.Info(\"Multi-Attach error: volume is already used by pods\", \"pods\", klog.KObjSlice(pods), \"attachedTo\", otherNodesStr, \"volume\", volumeToAttach)\n}\n","numLines":435,"startLine":1,"totalLines":435}}}

The registration chain works as follows:\\n\\n1. **Controller Registration via ControllerDescriptor** (cmd/kube-controller-manager/app/controllermanager.go:421-429): Each controller is wrapped in a `ControllerDescriptor` struct that contains the controller's name, initialization function (initFunc), required feature gates, and other metadata. Controllers are registered by calling a `register()` function within `NewControllerDescriptors()` (line 495).\\n\\n2. **Central Registration Point** (cmd/kube-controller-manager/app/controllermanager.go:495-593): The `NewControllerDescriptors()` function creates a map of all known controllers and registers them via the internal `register()` function. Each controller gets registered with validation to prevent duplicates and ensure proper initialization functions.\\n\\n3. **Manager-Level Controller Orchestration** (cmd/kube-controller-manager/app/controllermanager.go:661-767): The `StartControllers()` function iterates through registered controller descriptors and calls `StartController()` for each one. The `StartController()` function (line 708) executes the controller's initFunc with a `ControllerContext` that provides all necessary dependencies.\\n\\n4. **Dependency Injection via ControllerContext** (staging/src/k8s.io/controller-manager/app/controllercontext.go:29-62): Each controller receives a `ControllerContext` containing the ClientBuilder, InformerFactory, ObjectOrMetadataInformerFactory, RESTMapper, and other shared resources. The `StartController()` function (line 708) executes the controller's initFunc with a `ControllerContext` that provides all necessary dependencies.\\n\\n4. **Dependency Injection via ControllerContext** (staging/src/k8s.io/controller-manager/app/controllercontext.go:29-62): Each controller receives a `ControllerContext` containing the ClientBuilder, InformerFactory, ObjectOrMetadataInformerFactory, RESTMapper, and other shared resources. This is analogous to how a controller-runtime Manager injects dependencies into controllers.\\n\\n5. **Controller Interface Definition** (staging/src/k8s.io/controller-manager/controller/interfaces.go:25-55): Controllers implement the `controller.Interface` with a `Name()` method. Controllers can optionally implement `Debuggable` (for debugging handlers) and `HealthCheckable` (for health checks) interfaces.\\n\\n6. **Concrete Example: Deployment Controller Registration** (cmd/kube-controller-manager/app/apps.go:98-119): The `newDeploymentControllerDescriptor()` function creates a descriptor with the name and `startDeploymentController` as the initFunc. The `startDeploymentController()` function instantiates the deployment controller with informers and clients from the ControllerContext, then calls `Run()` on it to start the reconciliation loop.\\n\\n7. **Sample Controller Pattern** (staging/src/k8s.io/sample-controller/): Demonstrates the full controller implementation pattern with informer setup (controller.go:128-151) and the main controller loop that reconciles desired state with actual state (controller.go continues with syncHandler and other reconciliation methods).\\n\\nThe key difference from controller-runtime's explicit `SetupWithManager()` method is that Kubernetes uses an implicit registration pattern where controllers are discovered and initialized through the descriptor map, but the underlying concept is identical: controllers register their initialization functions with a central manager that provides context, orchestrates startup, and manages the lifecycle of the reconciliation loops.\"\n}\n","numLines":104,"startLine":1,"totalLines":104}}}
